            <script>
function scrollToAnchor(bookmark) {
    var $aTag = $("a[name='" + bookmark + "']");
    console.log("ScrollToAnchor called");
    console.log("Bookmark: " + bookmark);
    console.log("Objects: " + $aTag.length);
    if ($aTag.length) {
        console.log("Offset: " + $aTag.offset().top);
        $('html,body').animate({
            scrollTop: $aTag.offset().top
        }, 'slow');
    }
}

function scrollToDivById(div_id) {
    var $scrollDiv = $('#'+div_id);
    if ($scrollDiv) {
        $('html,body').delay(600).animate({
            scrollTop: $scrollDiv.position().top
        }, 'slow');
    }
}

function convertToName(label) {
    return label.replace(/'/g, "").replace(/and/g, "_").replace(/ /g, "").toLowerCase().trim();
}

function getParameterByName(name) {
    name = name.replace(/[\[]/, "\\[").replace(/&/g, "_").replace(/[\]]/, "\\]");
    var regex = new RegExp("[\\?&]" + name + "=([^&#]*)"),
        results = regex.exec(location.search);
    return results === null ? "" : decodeURIComponent(results[1].replace(/\+/g, " "));
}

function selectTabByName(tabToOpen, bookmark) {
    console.log ("STOFFEL IN selectTabByName with tabToOpen=" + tabToOpen);
    if (tabToOpen != "") {
        if (typeof(scrollToAnchor) == 'function') scrollToAnchor(bookmark);
        var classOfTabToOpen = '[class ^=' + convertToName(tabToOpen) + '][class $=_tab]';
        console.log("Tab to Open: " + classOfTabToOpen);
        var $tabByClassName = $(classOfTabToOpen);
        console.log("Length: " + $tabByClassName.length);
        if ($tabByClassName.length > 0) {
            // Found a class of a tab to open
            $tabByClassName.click();
        } else {
            $('.' + convertToName(tabToOpen)).click();
        }
    }
}

function selectTab(parentId, bookmark) {
	console.log ("STOFFEL IN selectTab with parentId=" + tabToOpen);
    // Assign a 'tab-name' to each tab
    $('#' + parentId).find('li a').each(function() {
        $(this).addClass(convertToName(($(this).attr('tabrender')).replace("HTML - ", "") + "_tab"));
    });
    $('.tab-content div[id$=_tab]').each(function() {
        $(this).addClass(convertToName(($(this).attr('tabrender')).replace("HTML - ", "")));
    });
    var tabToOpen = getParameterByName('tab');
    console.log(tabToOpen);
    selectTabByName(tabToOpen, bookmark);
}

function selectSubTab() {

    // CMK the subtab will be in the URL
    // once that item is found, then work backwards to ensure the containing tab is displayed, and then click it.
    var subTabToOpenString = getParameterByName('subtab');
    console.log ("STOFFEL IN selectSubTab with subTabToOpenString = "+subTabToOpenString);
    if (subTabToOpenString) {
    	console.log ("STOFFEL IN selectSubTab 2");
        var subTabToOpenAnchor = $('a[href="#' + subTabToOpenString + '"]');
        if (subTabToOpenAnchor) {
        	console.log ("STOFFEL IN selectSubTab 3");
            var parentIdString = subTabToOpenAnchor.data("parentid");
            if (parentIdString) {
            	console.log ("STOFFEL IN selectSubTab 4");
                // now get the link that is using this parent as its aria-control and click it, then click the subtab
								var parentTabToOpen = $('[aria-controls="' + parentIdString + '"]');
								// now if it's there, click it and click the subtab
								if(parentTabToOpen) {
									parentTabToOpen.click();
									subTabToOpenAnchor.click();
scrollToAnchor('productdetailtabs');
								}
            }
        }

    }
}
$(document).ready(function() {
  // now open the subtab if necessary.  Delay one second to allow for other tabs to build
  setTimeout(selectSubTab,500);
})
</script> 
            <!-- HTML - Common - Open Tab: End --> 
            <script class="tinkerScript">
  var prodCategories = "/Canon_NewWeb_Products/Products/product-categories/cameras/dslr/eos-70d";
  var prodName = "eos-70d";
  prodName = prodName.replace(/ /g, "+");

  // Get the valid product categories
  var categories = prodCategories.split(","); 
  var validCategories = [];
  var j = 0;
  for(i = 0; i < categories.length; i++){
    if((categories[i].indexOf(prodName) != -1) && (categories[i].indexOf("product-categories") != -1)) {
      validCategories[j] = categories[i];
      j++; 
    } 
  }

  //Iterate over whitepapers and remove the ones not directly relevant to the product
  $("tbody[id^='whitepaper_']").each(function(index, value) { 
    var dataCat = $(this).attr('data-cat'); 
    var whitepaperCategories = dataCat.split(",");

    var found = 'N';
    for(i = 0; (i < whitepaperCategories.length) && (found == 'N'); i++){
      for(j = 0; (j < validCategories.length) && (found == 'N'); j++){
        var paperCat = whitepaperCategories[i];
        var prodCat = validCategories[j];

        if(prodCat.indexOf(paperCat) > -1 ){
          // Found a product category that would have accepted this whitepaper
          found = 'Y';
        }
      }
    }
    if(found == 'Y') {
      found = 'N';
      var id = $(this).attr('id');
      $('#' + id).removeAttr("data-cat");
    }
    else {
      var id = $(this).attr('id'); 
      $('#' + id).remove(); 
    }
  });
  
  if($("tbody[id^='whitepaper']").length == 0) {
    $('#DataTables_Table_3').parent().empty();
  }
</script> 
            <script>

function setTabWidths (detailTabSelector, numberOfCurrentTabs) {        
        
	if (numberOfCurrentTabs==2) {
		tabColWidthClass = "col-sm-6" + " col-xs-6";
		$(detailTabSelector).removeClass("col-xs-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3").addClass(tabColWidthClass);

	} else if (numberOfCurrentTabs==3){
		tabColWidthClass = "col-sm-4" + " col-xs-12";
		$(detailTabSelector).removeClass("col-xs-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3").addClass(tabColWidthClass);

	} else if (numberOfCurrentTabs==4){
		tabColWidthClass = "col-sm-3" + " col-xs-6";
		$(detailTabSelector).removeClass("col-xs-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3").addClass(tabColWidthClass);

	} else if (numberOfCurrentTabs==5){
		tabColWidthClass = "col-sm-2 cf-offset-col-10 col-xs-12";
		$(detailTabSelector).removeClass("col-xs-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3").addClass(tabColWidthClass);

	} else if (numberOfCurrentTabs==6){
		tabColWidthClass = "col-sm-2" + " col-xs-6";
		$(detailTabSelector).removeClass("col-xs-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3").addClass(tabColWidthClass);

	} else if (numberOfCurrentTabs==7){
		tabColWidthClass = "col-sm-3 col-xs-12";
		$(detailTabSelector).removeClass("col-xs-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3").addClass(tabColWidthClass);
		$(detailTabSelector).slice(4).addClass("col-sm-4").removeClass('col-sm-3');

	} else if (numberOfCurrentTabs==8){
		tabColWidthClass = "col-sm-3" + " col-xs-6";
		$(detailTabSelector).removeClass("col-xs-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3").addClass(tabColWidthClass);

	} else if (numberOfCurrentTabs==9){
		tabColWidthClass = "col-xs-12";
		$(detailTabSelector).removeClass("col-xs-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3").addClass(tabColWidthClass);
		$(detailTabSelector).slice(0,5).addClass("col-sm-2 cf-offset-col-10");
		$(detailTabSelector).slice(5,9).addClass("col-sm-3");

	} else if (numberOfCurrentTabs==10){
		tabColWidthClass = "col-xs-6 col-sm-2 cf-offset-col-10";
		$(detailTabSelector).removeClass("col-xs-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3").addClass(tabColWidthClass);

	} else if (numberOfCurrentTabs==11){
		tabColWidthClass = "col-xs-12 col-sm-2";
		$(detailTabSelector).removeClass("col-xs-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3").addClass(tabColWidthClass);
		$(detailTabSelector).slice(6).addClass("col-sm-2 cf-offset-col-10 col-xs-12");

	} else if (numberOfCurrentTabs == 12){
		tabColWidthClass = "col-sm-2" + " col-xs-6";
		$(detailTabSelector).removeClass("col-xs-6 col-md-4 col-lg-3").addClass(tabColWidthClass);
	}

}

$(document).ready(function() {

	var detailTabSelector = "#db622c6c-8c97-4491-b020-71336d014529_OverviewTabs .detail-tabs";
	
	var numberOfCurrentTabs = $( detailTabSelector).length;
	console.log("CMK::"+numberOfCurrentTabs);
	setTabWidths (detailTabSelector, numberOfCurrentTabs);

});

</script>

            <script>
$( document ).ready(function() {

	function gotoTabNameFromAnchor() {
		// get hash from URL and decode if necessary
		var urlHash = window.location.hash;
		urlHash = $.trim(urlHash);
		if (urlHash.length == 0) {
			console.log("No Hash Found");
			return null;
		} 
		console.log("urlHash=" +urlHash);
		urlHash = urlHash.slice(1);
		urlHash = decodeURI(urlHash);
		console.log("urlHash=" +urlHash)
		
		// attempt to find matching tab 
		var tabSelector = "div[role='tabpanel'] .detail-tabs ."+urlHash;
		console.log ("tabSelector="+tabSelector);
		var $selectedTab = $(tabSelector).first();		
		var numberOfTabsFound = $selectedTab.length;
		
		console.log ("Found "+ numberOfTabsFound + " tab");
		if (numberOfTabsFound == 0) {
			return;
		} 
		console.log("Offset: " + $selectedTab.offset().top);
		
		// request to bootstrap tab to show
		$selectedTab.tab('show');
				
		var windowWidth = $( window ).width();
		console.log ("windowWidth="+windowWidth);
		if (windowWidth >= 768) {
			// desktop width: hide header, wait for completion of
			// transition, then scroll to tab
			// CMK 4/1/16 no longer need to add the class
			//$('header').removeClass('nav-down').addClass('nav-up');			
			$("header.site-header")
			.on("transitionend animationend webkitAnimationEnd oAnimationEnd MSAnimationEnd",
			function(e){
				console.log ("transition completed");
				console.log("Offset: " + $selectedTab.offset().top);
				$('html,body').animate({scrollTop: $selectedTab.offset().top},'slow');				
				$(this).off(e);
		 });
			
		} else {
			// mobile or tablet view; no need to remove 
			// nav bar, just scroll to tab
				$('html,body').animate({scrollTop: $selectedTab.offset().top},'slow');				
		
		}
				
		var tabHref = $selectedTab.attr("href");
		console.log("tabHref=" +tabHref);
		tabHref = tabHref.slice (1);
		//window.location.hash = tabHref;
		
		return;
	}
	  
  gotoTabNameFromAnchor();  
});
</script>

	//Set needed Coremetrics digitalData

	$(document).ready(function() {
		// Need to show ConfirmIt only on support pages
		if (window.location.href.indexOf("home/support") > -1) {
			var model = '';
			var category = '';
			if (window.location.href.indexOf("home/support/details") > -1) {
					var breadLength = digitalData.page.pageInfo.breadCrumbs.length;
					model = digitalData.page.pageInfo.breadCrumbs[breadLength - 1];
					category = digitalData.page.pageInfo.breadCrumbs[breadLength - 2];
			}					
			if (useMaritzCXSurvey == "N") {
				ConfirmIt
					.openSurvey(
							encodeURIComponent(model),
							encodeURIComponent(category));
			} else {
				
				McxSiteInterceptOnExit.addUrlParameter("mcxModel", model); 
				McxSiteInterceptOnExit.addUrlParameter("mcxPCategory", category);
				//Survey ID
				McxSiteInterceptOnExit.addUrlParameter("mcxID", "M6BSBQ");
				McxSiteInterceptOnExit.addUrlParameter("mcxReferrerURL", encodeURIComponent(window.location.href));
				McxSiteInterceptOnExit.acceptSurvey();
				//$('#surveyModal').modal('show');
				
			}
		}
	});
</script>
